TOOLKIT & METHODOLOGY\n\n## 3.1 TOOL SELECTION PRINCIPLES\n\n- IMAGE TOOL PRIORITY:\n  * For any request involving image creation, modification, style change, or visual design, ALWAYS prefer the Image Tool.\n  * Do NOT describe images purely in text when an image output is expected.\n  * If an image result is required, the Image Tool is mandatory.\n\n- CLI TOOLS PREFERENCE:\n  * Always prefer CLI tools over Python scripts when possible\n  * CLI tools are generally faster and more efficient for:\n    1. Integration with other Python code is necessary\n\n- HYBRID APPROACH: Combine Python and CLI as needed - use Python for logic and data processing, CLI for system operations and utilities\n\n## 3.2 CLI OPERATIONS BEST PRACTICES\n- Use terminal commands for system operations, file manipulations, and quick tasks\n- For command execution, you have two approaches:\n  1. Synchronous Commands (blocking):\n      * You can omit `blocking`, as it defaults to true\n      * Use for quick operations that complete within 60 seconds\n      * Commands run directly and wait for completion\n      * Example:\n        <function_calls>\n        <execute-command session_name="default" blocking="true">\n        ls -l\n        </execute-command>\n        </function_calls>\n        (or simply omit the blocking parameter as it defaults to true)\n      * IMPORTANT: Do not use for long-running operations as they will timeout after 60 seconds\n\n  2. Asynchronous Commands (non-blocking):\n      * Use `blocking="false"` for any command that might take longer than 60 seconds or for starting background services\n      * Commands run in background and return immediately\n      * Example:\n        <function_calls>\n        <execute-command session_name="dev" blocking="false">\n        npm run dev\n        </execute-command>\n        </function_calls>\n      * Common use cases:\n        - Development servers (Next.js, React, etc.)\n        - Build processes\n        - Long-running data processing\n        - Background services\n\n- Session Management:\n  * Each command must specify a session_name\n  * Use consistent session names for related commands\n  * Different sessions are isolated from each other\n  * Example: Use "build" session for build commands, "dev" for development servers\n  * Sessions maintain state between commands\n\n- Command Execution Guidelines:\n  * For commands that might take longer than 60 seconds, ALWAYS use run_async="true"\n  * Do not rely on increasing timeout for long-running commands\n  * Use proper session names for organization\n  * Chain commands with && for sequential execution\n  * Use | for piping output between commands\n  * Redirect output to files for long-running processes\n\n- Avoid commands requiring confirmation; actively use -y or -f flags for automatic confirmation\n- Avoid commands with excessive output; save to files when necessary\n- Chain multiple commands with operators to minimize interruptions and improve efficiency:\n  1. Use && for sequential execution: `command1 && command2 && command3`\n  2. Use || for fallback execution: `command1 || command2`\n  3. Use ; for unconditional execution: `command1; command2`\n  4. Use | for piping output: `command1 | command2`\n  5. Use > and >> for output redirection: `command > file` or `command >> file`\n- Use pipe operator to pass command outputs, simplifying operations\n- Use non-interactive `bc` for simple calculations, Python for complex math; never calculate mentally\n- Use `uptime` command when users explicitly request sandbox status check or wake-up\n\n## 3.3 CODE DEVELOPMENT PRACTICES\n- CODING:\n  * Must save code to files before execution; direct code input to interpreter commands is forbidden\n  * Write Python code for complex mathematical calculations and analysis\n  * Use search tools to find solutions when encountering unfamiliar problems\n  * For index.html, use deployment tools directly, or package everything into a zip file and provide it as a message attachment\n  * When creating web interfaces, always create CSS files first before HTML to ensure proper styling and design consistency\n  * For images, use real image URLs from sources like unsplash.com, pexels.com, pixabay.com, giphy.com, or wikimedia.org instead of creating placeholder images; use placeholder.com only as a last resort\n\n- WEBSITE DEPLOYMENT:\n  * Only use the \'deploy\' tool when users explicitly request permanent deployment to a production environment\n  * The deploy tool publishes static HTML+CSS+JS sites to a public URL using S3 web Pages\n  * If the same name is used for deployment, it will redeploy to the same project as before\n  * For temporary or development purposes, serve files locally instead of using the deployment tool\n  * When editing HTML files, always share the preview URL provided by the automatically running HTTP server with the user\n  * The preview URL is automatically generated and available in the tool results when creating or editing HTML files\n  * When deploying, ensure all assets (images, scripts, stylesheets) use relative paths to work correctly\n\n- PYTHON EXECUTION: Create reusable modules with proper error handling and logging. Use -i for case-insensitive\n    - Use -r for recursive search\n    - Use -A, -B, -C for context\n  2. awk: Column processing\n    - Use for structured data\n    - Use for data transformation\n  3. sed: Stream editing\n    - Use for text replacement\n    - Use for pattern matching\n- File Analysis:\n  1. file: Determine file type\n  2. wc: Count words/lines\n  3. head/tail: View file parts\n  4. less: View large files\n- Data Processing:\n  1. jq: JSON processing\n    - Use -n to specify number of lines\n    - Use -f to follow file changes\n  3. awk: Pattern scanning and processing\n    - Use for column-based data processing\n    - Use for complex text transformations\n  4. find: Locate files and directories\n    - Use -name for filename patterns\n    - Use -type for file types\n  5. wc: Word count and line counting\n    - Use -l for line count\n    - Use -w for word count\n    - Use -c for character count\n- Regex Patterns:\n  1. Use for precise text matching\n  2. Combine with CLI tools for powerful searches\n  3. Save complex patterns to files for reuse\n  4. Test patterns with small samples first\n  5. WORKFLOW MANAGEMENT\n\n## 5.1 AUTONOMOUS WORKFLOW SYSTEM\nYou operate through a self-maintained todo.md file that serves as your central source of truth and execution roadmap:\n\n1. Upon receiving a task, immediately create a lean, focused todo.md with essential sections covering the task lifecycle\n2. Each section contains specific, actionable subtasks based on complexity - use only as many as needed, no more\n3. Each task should be specific, actionable, and have clear completion criteria\n4. MUST actively work through these tasks one by one, checking them off as completed\n5. Adapt the plan as needed while maintaining its integrity as your execution compass\n\n## 5.2 TODO.MD FILE STRUCTURE AND USAGE\nThe todo.md file is your primary working document and action plan:\n\n1. Contains the complete list of tasks you MUST complete to fulfill the user\'s request\n2. Format with clear sections, each containing specific tasks marked with [ ] (incomplete) or [x] (complete)\n3. Each task should be specific, actionable, and have clear completion criteria\n4. MUST actively work through these tasks one by one, checking them off as completed\n5. Before every action, consult your todo.md to determine which task to tackle next\n6. The todo.md serves as your instruction set - if a task is in todo.md, you are responsible for completing it\n7. Update the todo.md as you make progress, adding new tasks as needed and marking completed ones\n8. Never delete tasks from todo.md - instead mark them complete with [x] to maintain a record of your work\n9. Once ALL tasks in todo.md are marked complete [x], you MUST call either the \'complete\' state or \'ask\' tool to signal task completion\n10. SCOPE CONSTRAINT: Focus on completing existing tasks before adding new ones; avoid continuously expanding scope\n11. CAPABILITY AWARENESS: Only add tasks that are achievable with your available tools and capabilities\n12. FINALITY: After marking a section complete, do not reopen it or add new tasks unless explicitly directed by the user\n13. STOPPING CONDITION: If you\'ve made 3 consecutive updates to todo.md without completing any tasks, reassess your approach and either simplify your plan or **use the \'ask\' tool to seek user guidance.**\n14. COMPLETION VERIFICATION: Only mark a task as [x] complete when you have concrete evidence of completion\n15. SIMPLICITY: Keep your todo.md lean and direct with clear actions, avoiding unnecessary verbosity or granularity\n\n## 5.3 EXECUTION PHILOSOPHY\nYour approach is deliberately methodical and persistent:\n\n1. Operate in a continuous loop until explicitly stopped\n2. Execute one step at a time, following a consistent loop: evaluate state → select tool → execute → provide narrative update → track progress\n3. Every action is guided by your todo.md, consulting it before selecting any tool\n4. Thoroughly verify each completed step before moving forward\n5. **Provide Markdown-formatted narrative updates directly in your responses** to keep the user informed of your progress, explain your thinking, and clarify the next steps. Use headers, brief descriptions, and context to make your process transparent.\n6. CRITICALLY IMPORTANT: Continue running in a loop until either:\n  - Using the **\'ask\' tool (THE ONLY TOOL THE USER CAN RESPOND TO)** to wait for essential user input (this pauses the loop)\n  - Using the \'complete\' tool when ALL tasks are finished\n7. For casual conversation:\n  - Use **\'ask\'** to properly end the conversation and wait for user input (**USER CAN RESPOND**)\n8. For tasks:\n  - Use **\'ask\'** when you need essential user input to proceed (**USER CAN RESPOND**)\n  - Provide **narrative updates** frequently in your responses to keep the user informed without requiring their input\n  - Use \'complete\' only when ALL tasks are finished\n9. MANDATORY COMPLETION:\n  - IMMEDIATELY use \'complete\' or \'ask\' after ALL tasks in todo.md are marked [x]\n  - NO additional commands or verifications after all tasks are complete\n  - NO further exploration or information gathering after completion\n  - NO redundant checks or validations after completion\n  - FAILURE to use \'complete\' or \'ask\' after task completion is a critical error\n\n## 5.4 TASK MANAGEMENT CYCLE\n1. STATE EVALUATION: Examine Todo.md for priorities, analyze recent Tool Results for environment understanding, and review past actions for context\n2. TOOL SELECTION: Choose exactly one tool that advances the current todo item\n3. EXECUTION: Wait for tool execution and observe results\n4. **NARRATIVE UPDATE:** Provide a **Markdown-formatted** narrative update directly in your response before the next tool call. Include explanations of what you\'ve done, what you\'re about to do, and why. Use headers, brief paragraphs, and formatting to enhance readability.\n5. PROGRESS TRACKING: Update todo.md with completed items and new tasks\n6. METHODICAL ITERATION: Repeat until section completion\n7. SECTION TRANSITION: Document completion and move to next section\n8. COMPLETION: IMMEDIATELY use \'complete\' or \'ask\' when ALL tasks are finished\n\n# 6. CONTENT CREATION\n\n## 6.1 WRITING GUIDELINES\n- Write content in continuous paragraphs using varied sentence lengths for engaging prose; avoid list formatting\n- Use prose and paragraphs by default; provide detailed content with proper citations\n- Strictly follow requirements in writing rules, and avoid using list formats in any files except todo.md\n\n## 6.2 DESIGN GUIDELINES\n- For any design-related task, first create the design in HTML+CSS to ensure maximum flexibility\n- Designs should be created with print-friendliness in mind - use appropriate margins, page breaks, and printable color schemes\n- After creating designs in HTML+CSS, convert directly to PDF as the final output format\n- When designing multi-page documents, ensure consistent styling and proper page numbering\n- Test print-readiness by confirming designs display correctly in print preview mode\n- For complex designs, test different media queries including print media type\n- Package all design assets (HTML, CSS, images, and PDF output) together when delivering final results\n- Ensure all fonts are properly embedded or use web-safe fonts to maintain design integrity in the PDF output\n- Set appropriate page sizes (A4, Letter, etc.) in the CSS using @page rules for consistent PDF rendering\n\n## Image Guidelines\n- ALWAYS use the Image Tool for image generation or image editing tasks\n- Write a single self-contained image prompt before calling the Image Tool\n- Clearly describe the main subject and overall composition\n- Explicitly specify the intended visual style and aesthetic\n- Provide exact text content if text is required; required\\\' });\\\\n    try {\\\\n        const user = await dbGet(\\\'SELECT username, wax_seal_path FROM users WHERE username = ?\\\', [name]);\\\\n        res.json({\\\\n            exists:  !!user,\\\\n            waxSeal: user?.wax_seal_path ? `/wax_seals/${user.wax_seal_path}` : null\\\\n        });\\\\n    } catch (e) { res.status(500).json({ error: \\\'Server error\\\' }); }\\\\n});\\\\n\\\\n/* Register */\\\\napp.post(\\\'/api/register\\\', async (req, res) => {\\\\n    const { name, password, confirmPassword, signatureData } = req.body;\\\\n\\\\n    if (!name) return res.status(400).json({ error: \\\'Name is required\\\' });\\\\n    if (!signatureData) return res.status(400).json({ error: \\\'Signature is required\\\' });\\\\n\\\\n    if (password) {\\\\n        if (password !== confirmPassword) return res.status(400).json({ error: \\\'Passwords do not match\\\' });\\\\n        const v = validatePassword(password);\\\\n        if (!v.valid) return res.status(400).json({ error: v.message });\\\\n    }\\\\n\\\\n    try {\\\\n        const existing = await dbGet(\\\'SELECT id FROM users WHERE username = ?\\\', [name]);\\\\n        if (existing) return res.status(400).json({ error: \\\'This name is already registered\\\' });\\\\n\\\\n        const hashed = password ? await bcrypt.hash(password, 12) : null;\\\\n        const token  = generateToken();\\\\n        const sealFile = await generateWaxSeal(name, signatureData);\\\\n\\\\n        await dbRun(\\\\n            `INSERT INTO users (username, password, unique_token, wax_seal_path, signature_data, signature_created_at)\\\\n             VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, datetime(\\\'now\\\'))`,\\\\n            [name, hashed, token, sealFile, JSON.stringify(signatureData)]\\\\n        );\\\\n\\\\n        req.session.userId   = (await dbGet(\\\'SELECT id FROM users WHERE username = ?\\\', [name])).id;\\\\n        req.session.userName = name;\\\\n\\\\n        res.json({ success: true, token, waxSeal: sealFile ? `/wax_seals/${sealFile}` : null });\\\\n    } catch (e) {\\\\n        console.error(\\\'Register error:\\\', e);\\\\n        res.status(500).json({ error: \\\'Registration failed: \\\' + e.message });\\\\n    }\\\\n});\\\\n\\\\n/* Login */\\\\napp.post(\\\'/api/login\\\', async (req, res) => {\\\\n    const { name, password, signatureData } = req.body;\\\\n    if (!name) return res.status(400).json({ error: \\\'Name required\\\' });\\\\n\\\\n    try {\\\\n        const user = await dbGet(\\\'SELECT * FROM users WHERE username = ?\\\', [name]);\\\\n        if (!user) return res.status(401).json({ error: \\\'No account found with that name\\\' });\\\\n\\\\n        /* Signature-first auth */\\\\n        if (signatureData && user.signature_data) {\\\\n            const result = sigVerifier.verifySignature(signatureData, user.signature_data);\\\\n            if (result.success) {\\\\n                req.session.userId   = user.id;\\\\n                req.session.userName = user.username;\\\\n                return res.json({\\\\n                    success: true, authMethod: \\\'signature\\\',\\\\n                    confidence: result.confidence,\\\\n                    token:   user.unique_token,\\\\n                    waxSeal: user.wax_seal_path ? `/wax_seals/${user.wax_seal_path}` : null\\\\n                });\\\\n            }\\\\n            /* Signature failed \\\\u2014 try password fallback */\\\\n            if (password && user.password) {\\\\n                const ok = await bcrypt.compare(password, user.password);\\\\n                if (ok) {\\\\n                    req.session.userId   = user.id;\\\\n                    req.session.userName = user.username;\\\\n                    return res.json({\\\\n                        success: true, authMethod: \\\'password\\\',\\\\n                        message: \\\'Signature did not match; password backup accepted\\\',\\\\n                        token:   user.unique_token,\\\\n                        waxSeal: user.wax_seal_path ? `/wax_seals/${user.wax_seal_path}` : null\\\\n                    });\\\\n                }\\\\n            }\\\\n            return res.status(401).json({\\\\n                error:      \\\'Signature verification failed\\\',\\\\n                confidence: result.confidence,\\\\n                threshold:  result.threshold,\\\\n                message:    \\\'Please retry or use your backup password\\\'\\\\n            });\\\\n        }\\\\n\\\\n        /* Password-only path */\\\\n        if (password && user.password) {\\\\n            const ok = await bcrypt.compare(password, user.password);\\\\n            if (ok) {\\\\n                req.session.userId   = user.id;\\\\n                req.session.userName = user.username;\\\\n                return res.json({\\\\n                    success: true, authMethod: \\\'password\\\',\\\\n                    token:   user.unique_token,\\\\n                    waxSeal: user.wax_seal_path ? `/wax_seals/${user.wax_seal_path}` : null\\\\n                });\\\\n            }\\\\n            return res.status(401).json({ error: \\\'Incorrect password\\\' });\\\\n        }\\\\n\\\\n        res.status(401).json({ error: \\\'Please provide your signature or password\\\', hasPassword: !!user.password });\\\\n    } catch (e) {\\\\n        console.error(\\\'Login error:\\\', e);\\\\n        res.status(500).json({ error: \\\'Login failed\\\' });\\\\n    }\\\\n});\\\\n\\\\n/* Check if current session is admin */\\\\napp.get(\\\'/api/admin/check-auth\\\', (req, res) => {\\\\n    if (req.session && req.session.isAdmin) {\\\\n        res.json({ authenticated: true });\\\\n    } else {\\\\n        res.status(401).json({ authenticated: false });\\\\n    }\\\\n});\\\\n\\\\n/* Get full agreement detail for owner });\\\\n});\\\\n\\\\n/* \\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\n \\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550     ).join(\\\'\\\\\\\\n\\\');\\\\n\\\\n        const scriptContent = `\\\\nimport sys\\\\nsys.path.insert(0, \\\'/workspace\\\')\\\\nimport os\\\\nos.chdir(\\\'/workspace\\\')\\\\n\\\\n# Override    perUserMonthly: 25\\\\n            }\\\\n        ]\\\\n    }\\\\n];\\\\n\\\\n/* --- CLOUD STAGE RENDERING ----------------------------------------------- */\\\\nfunction showCloudStage(stageIndex) {\\\\n    const stage = cloudTree[stageIndex];\\\\n    if (!stage) return;\\\\n\\\\n    state.currentStageIndex = stageIndex;\\\\n\\\\n    const cloudStageEl = document.getElementById(\\\'cloud-stage\\\');\\\\n    const backBtn = document.getElementById(\\\'back-btn\\\');\\\\n    const nextPreview = document.getElementById(\\\'next-preview\\\');\\\\n    const progressFill = document.getElementById(\\\'progress-fill\\\');\\\\n\\\\n    // Back button\\\\n    if (backBtn) backBtn.style.display = state.cloudHistory.length > 0 ? \\\'block\\\' : \\\'none\\\';\\\\n\\\\n    // Progress bar\\\\n    if (progressFill) {\\\\n        const progress = Math.min(100, (stageIndex / (cloudTree.length - 1)) * 100);\\\\n        progressFill.style.width = progress + \\\'%\\\';\\\\n    }\\\\n\\\\n    // Next stage preview\\\\n    if (nextPreview && stage.options[0]) {\\\\n        const ns = stage.options[0].nextStage;\\\\n        if (ns === \\\'complete\\\') {\\\\n            nextPreview.textContent = \\\'Final step \\\\u2014 review and generate your agreement\\\';\\\\n        } else {\\\\n            const found = cloudTree.find(s => s.id === ns);\\\\n            nextPreview.textContent = found ? \\\'Up next: \\\' + found.title : \\\'\\\';\\\\n        }\\\\n    }\\\\n\\\\n    // Update topbar username\\\\n    const configUser = document.getElementById(\\\'config-username\\\');\\\\n    if (configUser && state.userName) configUser.textContent = state.userName + \\\\"\\\'s Configuration\\\\";\\\\n\\\\n    // Update topbar seal\\\\n    const topbarSeal = document.getElementById(\\\'topbar-seal\\\');\\\\n    if (topbarSeal && state.waxSealImage) topbarSeal.src = state.waxSealImage;\\\\n\\\\n    // Render stage\\\\n    cloudStageEl.innerHTML = `\\\\n        <div class=\\\\"cloud-stage-inner\\\\">\\\\n            <div class=\\\\"stage-header\\\\">\\\\n                <div class=\\\\"stage-icon\\\\">${stage.icon || \\\'\\\'}</div>\\\\n                <h2>${stage.title}</h2>\\\\n                <p class=\\\\"stage-desc\\\\">${stage.description}</p>\\\\n            </div>\\\\n            <div class=\\\\"cloud-options-grid\\\\">\\\\n                ${stage.options.map(opt => `\\\\n                    <div class=\\\\"cloud-option\\\\" data-option-id=\\\\"${opt.id}\\\\" data-stage-id=\\\\"${stage.id}\\\\">\\\\n                        <div class=\\\\"cloud-opt-icon\\\\">${opt.icon || \\\'\\\\u25c6\\\'}</div>\\\\n                        <h3>${opt.title}</h3>\\\\n                        <p class=\\\\"cloud-opt-desc\\\\">${opt.details}</p>\\\\n                        <div class=\\\\"cloud-opt-price\\\\">${opt.price}</div>\\\\n                    </div>\\\\n                `).join(\\\'\\\')}\\\\n            </div>\\\\n        </div>\\\\n    `;\\\\n\\\\n    // Attach click handlers\\\\n    cloudStageEl.querySelectorAll(\\\'.cloud-option\\\').forEach(el => {\\\\n        el.addEventListener(\\\'click\\\', () => handleCloudOption(stage.id, el.dataset.optionId));\\\\n    });\\\\n}\\\\n\\\\nfunction handleCloudOption(stageId, optionId) {\\\\n    const stage = cloudTree.find(s => s.id === stageId);\\\\n    if (!stage) return;\\\\n    const selectedOption = stage.options.find(o => o.id === optionId);\\\\n    if (!selectedOption) return;\\\\n\\\\n    // Store selection\\\\n    state.preferences[stageId] = { ...selectedOption };\\\\n\\\\n    // History\\\\n    state.cloudHistory.push({ stageId: stageId, stageIndex: state.currentStageIndex, optionId });\\\\n\\\\n    // Persist\\\\n    fetch(\\\'/api/preferences\\\', {\\\\n        method: \\\'POST\\\',\\\\n        headers: { \\\'Content-Type\\\': \\\'application/json\\\' },\\\\n        body: JSON.stringify({ preferences: state.preferences })\\\\n    }).catch(() => {});\\\\n\\\\n    // Navigate\\\\n    if (selectedOption.nextStage === \\\'complete\\\') {\\\\n        buildAndShowAgreement();\\\\n    } else {\\\\n        const nextIndex = cloudTree.findIndex(s => s.id === selectedOption.nextStage);\\\\n        if (nextIndex >= 0) showCloudStage(nextIndex);\\\\n    }\\\\n}\\\\n\\\\n// Back navigation\\\\ndocument.getElementById(\\\'back-btn\\\').addEventListener(\\\'click\\\', () => {\\\\n    if (state.cloudHistory.length > 0) {\\\\n        const last = state.cloudHistory.pop();\\\\n        delete state.preferences[last.stageId];\\\\n        fetch(\\\'/api/preferences\\\', {\\\\n            method: \\\'POST\\\',\\\\n            headers: { \\\'Content-Type\\\': \\\'application/json\\\' },\\\\n            body: JSON.stringify({ preferences: state.preferences })\\\\n        }).catch(() => {});\\\\n        showCloudStage(last.stageIndex);\\\\n    }\\\\n});\\\\n\\\\n/* --- LANDING PAGE --------------------------------------------------------- */\\\\nfunction handleNameEntry() {\\\\n    const input = document.getElementById(\\\'name-input\\\');\\\\n    const name = input ? input.value.trim() : \\\'\\\';\\\\n    if (!name) { alert(\\\'Please enter your full name\\\'); return; }\\\\n    state.userName = name;\\\\n\\\\n    fetch(\\\'/api/check-user\\\', {\\\\n        method: \\\'POST\\\',\\\\n        headers: { \\\'Content-Type\\\': \\\'application/json\\\' },\\\\n        body: JSON.stringify({ name })\\\\n    })\\\\n    .then(r => r.json())\\\\n    .then(data => {\\\\n        if (data.exists) {\\\\n            const seal = document.getElementById(\\\'login-wax-seal\\\');\\\\n            if (seal) seal.src = data.waxSeal || \\\'\\\';\\\\n            showPage(\\\'login-page\\\');\\\\n            initLoginSigPad();\\\\n        } else {\\\\n            showPage(\\\'password-page\\\');\\\\n            startSealGeneration();\\\\n        }\\\\n    })\\\\n    .catch(() => {\\\\n        showPage(\\\'password-page\\\');\\\\n        startSealGeneration();\\\\n    });\\\\n}\\\\n\\\\ndocument.getElementById(\\\'name-input\\\').addEventListener(\\\'keypress\\\', e => {\\\\n    if (e.key === \\\'Enter\\\') handleNameEntry();\\\\n});\\\\ndocument.getElementById(\\\'enter-name-btn\\\').addEventListener(\\\'click\\\', handleNameEntry);\\\\n\\\\n/* --- REGISTRATION --------------------------------------------------------- */\\\\nfunction startSealGeneration() {\\\\n    const generating = document.getElementById(\\\'seal-generating\\\');\\\\n    const form = document.getElementById(\\\'signature-password-form\\\');\\\\n    const result = document.getElementById(\\\'wax-seal-result\\\');\\\\n    if (generating) generating.style.display = \\\'flex\\\';\\\\n    if (form) form.style.display = \\\'none\\\';\\\\n    if (result) result.style.display = \\\'none\\\';\\\\n\\\\n    setTimeout(() => {\\\\n        if (generating) generating.style.display = \\\'none\\\';\\\\n        if (form) form.style.display = \\\'block\\\';\\\\n        initRegisterSigPad();\\\\n    }, 3000);\\\\n}\\\\n\\\\n/* --- SIGNATURE PAD FACTORY ----------------------------------------------- */\\\\nfunction createSigPad(canvas) {\\\\n    const ctx = canvas.getContext(\\\'2d\\\');\\\\n    ctx.strokeStyle = \\\'#1a1a2e\\\';\\\\n    ctx.lineWidth = 2.2;\\\\n    ctx.lineCap = \\\'round\\\';\\\\n    ctx.lineJoin = \\\'round\\\';\\\\n\\\\n    let drawing = false;\\\\n    let pts = [];\\\\n    let lastX = 0, lastY = 0;\\\\n\\\\n    function coords(e) {\\\\n        const r = canvas.getBoundingClientRect();\\\\n        const src = e.touches ? e.touches[0] : e;\\\\n        return [src.clientX - r.left, src.clientY - r.top];\\\\n    }\\\\n    function down(e) {\\\\n        e.preventDefault();\\\\n        drawing = true;\\\\n        [lastX, lastY] = coords(e);\\\\n        pts.push({ x: lastX, y: lastY, t: Date.now() });\\\\n    }\\\\n    function move(e) {\\\\n        if (!drawing) return;\\\\n        e.preventDefault();\\\\n        const [x, y] = coords(e);\\\\n        ctx.beginPath();\\\\n        ctx.moveTo(lastX, lastY);\\\\n        ctx.lineTo(x, y);\\\\n        ctx.stroke();\\\\n        [lastX, lastY] = [x, y];\\\\n        pts.push({ x, y, t: Date.now() });\\\\n    }\\\\n    function up() { drawing = false; }\\\\n\\\\n    canvas.addEventListener(\\\'mousedown\\\', down);\\\\n    canvas.addEventListener(\\\'mousemove\\\', move);\\\\n    canvas.addEventListener(\\\'mouseup\\\', up);\\\\n    canvas.addEventListener(\\\'mouseout\\\', up);\\\\n    canvas.addEventListener(\\\'touchstart\\\', down, { passive: false });\\\\n    canvas.addEventListener(\\\'touchmove\\\', move, { passive: false });\\\\n    canvas.addEventListener(\\\'touchend\\\', up);\\\\n\\\\n    return {\\\\n        clear() { ctx.clearRect(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height); pts = []; },\\\\n        getData() { return pts.length > 8 ? pts : null; },\\\\n        getImage() { return canvas.toDataURL(\\\'image/png\\\'); }\\\\n    };\\\\n}\\\\n\\\\nfunction initRegisterSigPad() {\\\\n    const canvas = document.getElementById(\\\'register-signature-pad\\\');\\\\n    if (!canvas) return;\\\\n    state.registerSigPad = createSigPad(canvas);\\\\n    document.getElementById(\\\'clear-register-signature\\\').addEventListener(\\\'click\\\', () => {\\\\n        if (state.registerSigPad) state.registerSigPad.clear();\\\\n showPage(\\\'cloud-page\\\');\\\\n            showCloudStage(0);\\\\n        });\\\\n}\\\\n\\\\n/* --- AGREEMENT BUILDER ---------------------------------------------------- */\\\\nfunction computeTotalLabel() {\\\\n    let base = 0;\\\\n    let monthly = 0;\\\\n\\\\n    // Base project cost\\\\n    const pt = state.preferences[\\\'project-type\\\'];\\\\n    if (pt && pt.basePrice) base += pt.basePrice;\\\\n    const wt = state.preferences[\\\'website-type\\\'];\\\\n    if (wt && wt.basePrice) base += wt.basePrice;\\\\n    const st = state.preferences[\\\'server-type\\\'];\\\\n    if (st && st.basePrice) base += st.basePrice;\\\\n    const stt = state.preferences[\\\'startup-type\\\'];\\\\n    if (stt && stt.basePrice) base += stt.basePrice;\\\\n\\\\n    // Addon one-time costs\\\\n    const wf = state.preferences[\\\'website-features\\\'];\\\\n    if (wf && wf.addonPrice) base += wf.addonPrice;\\\\n    const sa = state.preferences[\\\'server-addons\\\'];\\\\n    if (sa && sa.addonPrice) monthly += sa.addonPrice;\\\\n    const sta = state.preferences[\\\'startup-addons\\\'];\\\\n    if (sta && sta.addonPrice) base += sta.addonPrice;\\\\n\\\\n    // Hosting\\\\n    const hosting = state.preferences[\\\'hosting\\\'];\\\\n    if (hosting && hosting.monthlyAddon) monthly += hosting.monthlyAddon;\\\\n\\\\n    // Ownership\\\\n    const own = state.preferences[\\\'ownership\\\'];\\\\n    if (own && own.monthly) monthly += own.monthly;\\\\n\\\\n    // AI\\\\n    const ai = state.preferences[\\\'ai\\\'];\\\\n    if (ai && ai.aiAddon) monthly += ai.aiAddon;\\\\n\\\\n    // Maintenance\\\\n    const maint = state.preferences[\\\'maintenance\\\'];\\\\n    if (maint && maint.maintenanceAddon) monthly += maint.maintenanceAddon;\\\\n\\\\n    // Addons\\\\n    const addons = state.preferences[\\\'addons\\\'];\\\\n    if (addons) {\\\\n        if (addons.addonOneTime) base += addons.addonOneTime;\\\\n        if (addons.addonMonthly) monthly += addons.addonMonthly;\\\\n    }\\\\n\\\\n    // ETA Rush surcharge\\\\n    const eta = state.preferences[\\\'eta-rush\\\'];\\\\n    if (eta && eta.etaMultiplier && eta.etaMultiplier > 0) {\\\\n        const surcharge = Math.round(base * eta.etaMultiplier);\\\\n        base += surcharge;\\\\n    }\\\\n    if (eta && eta.perUserMonthly) {\\\\n        monthly += eta.perUserMonthly; // per-user base estimate\\\\n    }\\\\n\\\\n    let label = \\\'\\\';\\\\n    if (base > 0) label += `Est. $${base.toLocaleString()} CAD one-time`;\\\\n    if (monthly > 0) label += (label ? \\\' + \\\' : \\\'\\\') + `$${monthly.toLocaleString()}/mo`;\\\\n    return label || \\\'Custom pricing \\\\u2014 contact for quote\\\';\\\\n}\\\\n\\\\nfunction buildAndShowAgreement() {\\\\n    const prefs = Agreement\\\';\\\\n        return \\\'Custom Development Agreement\\\';\\\\n    })();\\\\n\\\\n    state.agreementData.type = agType;\\\\n    state.agreementData.totalLabel = totalLabel;\\\\n\\\\n 0.5) * 0.4,\n        vy: (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.4,\n        a: Math.random() * Math.PI * 2,\n        hue: Math.floor(Math.random() * 3),\n        colors: [\'rgba(245,200,66,\', \'rgba(0,229,255,\', \'rgba(168,85,247,\']\n    }));\n\n    function draw() {\n        ctx.clearRect(0, 0, W, H);\n\n        // Mouse nebula glow\n        const grd = ctx.createRadialGradient(mouseX, mouseY, 0, mouseX, mouseY, 180);\n        grd.addColorStop(0, \'rgba(168,85,247,0.08)\');\n        grd.addColorStop(0.5, \'rgba(0,229,255,0.04)\');\n        grd.addColorStop(1, \'rgba(0,0,0,0)\');\n        ctx.fillStyle = grd;\n        ctx.fillRect(0, 0, W, H);\n\n        particles.forEach(p => {\n            const dx = mouseX - p.x, dy = mouseY - p.y;\n            const dist = Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy);\n            if (dist < 200) {\n                p.vx += dx * 0.00004;\n                p.vy += dy * 0.00004;\n            }\n            const speed = Math.sqrt(p.vx * p.vx + p.vy * p.vy);\n            if (speed > 0.8) { p.vx *= 0.8 / speed; p.vy *= 0.8 / speed; }\n\n            p.x += p.vx; p.y += p.vy;\n            p.a += 0.006;\n            if (p.x < 0) p.x = W; if (p.x > W) p.x = 0;\n            if (p.y < 0) p.y = H; if (p.y > H) p.y = 0;\n            const alpha = (Math.sin(p.a) * 0.4 + 0.5) * 0.75;\n            ctx.beginPath();\n            ctx.arc(p.x, p.y, p.r, 0, Math.PI * 2);\n            ctx.fillStyle = p.colors[p.hue] + alpha + \')\';\n            ctx.fill();\n        });\n        requestAnimationFrame(draw);\n    }\n    draw();\n    window.addEventListener(\'resize\', () => {\n        W = canvas.width = window.innerWidth;\n        H = canvas.height = window.innerHeight;\n    });\n})();\n\n/* --- PARALLAX / PSYCHEDELIC HERO ----------------------------------------- */\n(function initParallax() {\n    let targetX = 0, targetY = 0, curX = 0, curY = 0;\n    let hueShift = 0;\n\n    document.addEventListener(\'mousemove\', e => {\n        targetX = (e.clientX / window.innerWidth  - 0.5) * 30;\n        targetY = (e.clientY / window.innerHeight - 0.5) * 20;\n        hueShift = (e.clientX / window.innerWidth) * 60;\n    });\n\n    function loop() {\n        curX += (targetX - curX) * 0.06;\n        curY += (targetY - curY) * 0.06;\n\n        const hero = document.querySelector(\'.landing-hero\');\n        const rings = document.querySelectorAll(\'.outer-ring\');\n        const mascotWrap = document.querySelector(\'.mascot-seal-wrapper\');\n\n        if (hero) {\n            hero.style.transform = `translate(${curX * 0.3}px, ${curY * 0.2}px)`;\n        }\n        if (mascotWrap) {\n            mascotWrap.style.transform = `translate(${curX * 0.6}px, ${curY * 0.5}px)`;\n        }\n\n        rings.forEach((ring, i) => {\n            const depth = (i + 1) * 0.25;\n            ring.style.transform = `translate(-50%, -50%) translate(${curX * depth}px, ${curY * depth}px)`;\n            const h = Math.round(hueShift + i * 20) % 360;\n            ring.style.boxShadow = `0 0 ${18 + i * 8}px hsla(${h},90%,60%,0.4), inset 0 0 ${10 + i * 5}px hsla(${h},90%,60%,0.15)`;\n        });\n\n        requestAnimationFrame(loop);\n    }\n    loop();\n})();\n\n/* --- PAGE NAVIGATION ------------------------------------------------------ */\nfunction showPage(pageId) {\n    document.querySelectorAll(\'.page\').forEach(p => p.classList.remove(\'active\'));\n    const target = document.getElementById(pageId);\n    if (target) target.classList.add(\'active\');\n    state.currentPage = pageId;\n}\n\n/* ==========================================================================\n   CLOUD CONFIGURATION TREE — Structured Pricing Engine\n   All prices use: oneTimeMin, oneTimeMax, monthlyMin, monthlyMax,\n                   hourly, perUserMonthly, percentOfOneTime\n   ========================================================================== */\n\nconst cloudTree = [\n    {\n        id: \'project-type\',\n        title: \'What Are We Building?\',\n        icon: \'🏗️\',\n        description: \'Select the primary type of solution you need. Timeline varies by project complexity — typically 2-6 months.\',\n                oneTimeMin: 0, oneTimeMax: 0, monthlyMin: 0, monthlyMax: 0,\n                etaMultiplier: 0\n            },\n            {\n                id: \'rush-level2\',\n                icon: \'⚡\',\n                title: \'Rush Level 2 — 3 to 7 Months\',\n                price: \'+18% of project total\',\n                nextStage: \'review\',\n                details: \'Accelerated delivery with priority scheduling. Dedicated team allocation ensures 3-7 month completion.\',\n                oneTimeMin: 0, oneTimeMax: 0, monthlyMin: 0, monthlyMax: 0,\n                etaMultiplier: 0.18, percentOfOneTime: 18\n            },\n            {\n                id: \'rush-level3\',\n                icon: \'🔥\',\n                title: \'Rush Level 3 — 2 to 3 Months\',\n                price: \'+35% of project total\',\n                nextStage: \'review\',\n                details: \'High-priority fast-track delivery. Extended hours, dedicated resources, weekly milestone reviews.\',\n                oneTimeMin: 0, oneTimeMax: 0, monthlyMin: 0, monthlyMax: 0,\n                etaMultiplier: 0.35, percentOfOneTime: 35\n            },\n            {\n                id: \'premiere-enterprise\',\n                icon: \'👑\',\n                title: \'Première Enterprise — 1-Week Demo\',\n                price: \'+65% upfront + $25/user/mo\',\n                nextStage: \'premiere-config\',\n                details: \'Demo version delivered within 1 week. Your company runs on the beta platform immediately while the full build continues. $25/user/month billing applies until build completion.\',\n                oneTimeMin: 0, oneTimeMax: 0, monthlyMin: 0, monthlyMax: 0,\n                etaMultiplier: 0.65, percentOfOneTime: 65, perUserMonthly: 25\n            }\n        ]\n    },\n\n    /* —— PREMIÈRE ENTERPRISE CONFIG —— */\n    {\n        id: \'premiere-config\',\n        title: \'Première Enterprise Setup\',\n        icon: \'👑\',\n        description: \'Configure your enterprise demo deployment. Tell us about your team and login requirements.\',\n        isConditional: true,\n        options: []\n    },\n\n    /* —— REVIEW / CART STAGE —— */\n    {\n        id: \'review\',\n        title: \'Review Your Configuration\',\n        icon: \'📋\',\n        description: \'Review all your selections before proceeding to the agreement. Click any item to edit.\',\n        isReview: true,\n        options: []\n    }\n];\n\n/* --- CLOUD STAGE RENDERING ----------------------------------------------- */\nfunction showCloudStage(stageIndex) {\n    const stage = cloudTree[stageIndex];\n    if (!stage) return;\n\n    state.currentStageIndex = stageIndex;\n\n    const cloudStageEl = document.getElementById(\'cloud-stage\');\n    const backBtn = document.getElementById(\'back-btn\');\n    const nextPreview = document.getElementById(\'next-preview\');\n    const progressFill = document.getElementById(\'progress-fill\');\n\n    // Back button\n    if (backBtn) backBtn.style.display = state.cloudHistory.length > 0 ? \'block\' : \'none\';\n\n    // Progress bar\n    if (progressFill) {\n        const progress = Math.min(100, (stageIndex / (cloudTree.length - 1)) * 100);\n        progressFill.style.width = progress + \'%\';\n    }\n\n    // Next stage preview\n    if (nextPreview && stage.options && stage.options[0]) {\n        const ns = stage.options[0].nextStage;\n        if (ns === \'review\') {\n            nextPreview.textContent = \'Next: Review your configuration before agreement\';\n        } else {\n            const found = cloudTree.find(s => s.id === ns);\n            nextPreview.textContent = found ? \'Up next: \' + found.title : \'\';\n        }\n    } else if (nextPreview) {\n        nextPreview.textContent = \'\';\n    }\n\n    // Update topbar username\n    const configUser = document.getElementById(\'config-username\');\n    if (configUser && state.userName) configUser.textContent = state.userName + "\'s Configuration";\n\n    // Update topbar seal\n    const topbarSeal = document.getElementById(\'topbar-seal\');\n    if (topbarSeal && state.waxSealImage) topbarSeal.src = state.waxSealImage;\n\n    // Handle special stages\n    if (stage.isConditional && stage.id === \'premiere-config\') {\n        renderPremiereConfig(cloudStageEl);\n        return;\n    }\n    if (stage.isReview) {\n        renderReviewStage(cloudStageEl);\n        return;\n    }\n\n    // Render normal stage\n    cloudStageEl.innerHTML = `\n        <div class="cloud-stage-inner">\n            <div class="stage-header">\n                <div class="stage-icon">${stage.icon || \'\'}</div>\n                <h2>${stage.title}</h2>\n                <p class="stage-desc">${stage.description}</p>\n            </div>\n            <div class="cloud-options-grid">\n                ${stage.options.map(opt => `\n                    <div class="cloud-option" data-option-id="${opt.id}" data-stage-id="${stage.id}">\n                        <div class="cloud-opt-icon">${opt.icon || \'◆\'}</div>\n                        <h3>${opt.title}</h3>\n                        <p class="cloud-opt-desc">${opt.details}</p>\n                        <div class="cloud-opt-price">${opt.price}</div>\n                    </div>\n                `).join(\'\')}\n            </div>\n        </div>\n    `;\n\n    // Attach click handlers\n    cloudStageEl.querySelectorAll(\'.cloud-option\').forEach(el => {\n        el.addEventListener(\'click\', () => handleCloudOption(stage.id, el.dataset.optionId));\n    });\n}\n\n/* --- PREMIÈRE ENTERPRISE CONFIG RENDERER --------------------------------- */\nfunction          <h2>Première Enterprise Setup</h2>\n                <p class="stage-desc">Configure your enterprise demo deployment. \'active\' : \'\'}" data-val="no">\n                            <span class="toggle-icon">🚪</span> No — Open Access\n                        </button>\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="premiere-field" id="premiere-user-count-field" style="display:${state.premiereNeedsLogins ? \'block\' : \'none\'}">\n                    <label class="premiere-label">How many users will need access?</label>\n                    <div class="premiere-slider-wrap">\n                        <input type="range" id="premiere-user-slider" min="1" max="200" value="${state.premiereUsers}" class="premiere-slider">\n                        <div class="premiere-user-display">\n                            <span class="user-count-num" id="premiere-user-num">${state.premiereUsers}</span>\n                            <span class="user-count-label">users</span>\n                        </div>\n                        <div class="premiere-cost-preview" id="premiere-cost-preview">\n                            $${state.premiereUsers * 25}/month user billing\n                        </div>\n                    </div>\n                    <div class="glow-input-wrap" style="max-width:200px;margin-top:12px;">\n                        <input type="number" id="premiere-user-exact" min="1" max="500" value="${state.premiereUsers}" placeholder="Exact count">\n                        <div class="input-glow-line"></div>\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n                <div class="premiere-summary">\n                    <div class="premiere-summary-line">\n                        <span>Rush Surcharge:</span>\n                        <span class="premiere-val">+65% of project total</span>\n                    </div>\n                    <div class="premiere-summary-line" id="premiere-monthly-line" style="display:${state.premiereNeedsLogins ? \'block\' : \'none\';\n            if (monthlyLine) monthlyLine.style.display = state.premiereNeedsLogins ? \'flex\' : \'none\';\n        });\n    });\n\n    // Slider handler\n    const slider = document.getElementById(\'premiere-user-slider\');\n    const exactInput = document.getElementById(\'premiere-user-exact\');\n    const numDisplay = document.getElementById(\'premiere-user-num\');\n    const costPreview = document.getElementById(\'premiere-cost-preview\');\n    const monthlyVal = document.getElementById(\'premiere-monthly-val\');\n\n    function updateUserCount(val) {\n        val = Math.max(1, Math.min(500, parseInt(val) || 1));\n        state.premiereUsers = val;\n        if (numDisplay) numDisplay.textContent = val;\n        if (costPreview) costPreview.textContent = `$${val * 25}/month user billing`;\n        if (monthlyVal) monthlyVal.textContent = `$${val * 25}/mo until completion`;\n        if (slider && parseInt(slider.value) !== val) slider.value = Math.min(val, 200);\n        if (exactInput && parseInt(exactInput.value) !== val) exactInput.value = val;\n    }\n\n    if (slider) slider.addEventListener(\'input\', () => updateUserCount(slider.value));\n    if (exactInput) exactInput.addEventListener(\'input\', () => updateUserCount(exactInput.value));\n\n    // Continue button\n    document.getElementById(\'premiere-continue-btn\').addEventListener(\'click\', () => {\n        // Store premiere config in preferences\n        state.preferences[\'premiere-config\'] = {\n            id: \'premiere-config\',\n            title: \'Première Enterprise Config\',\n            price: state.premiereNeedsLogins ? `$${state.premiereUsers * 25}/mo (${state.premiereUsers} users)` : \'Open access — no per-user billing\',\n            details: state.premiereNeedsLogins\n                ? `${state.premiereUsers} user accounts with login access at $25/user/month until build completion.`\n                : \'Open access mode — no individual user accounts required.\',\n            needsLogins: state.premiereNeedsLogins,\n            userCount: state.premiereNeedsLogins ? state.premiereUsers : 0,\n            perUserMonthly: state.premiereNeedsLogins ? 25 : 0,\n            oneTimeMin: 0, oneTimeMax: 0,\n            monthlyMin: state.premiereNeedsLogins ? state.premiereUsers * 25 : 0,\n            monthlyMax: state.premiereNeedsLogins ? state.premiereUsers * 25 : 0\n        };\n\n        state.cloudHistory.push({ stageId: \'premiere-config\', stageIndex: state.currentStageIndex, optionId: \'premiere-config\' });\n\n        // Persist\n        fetch(\'/api/preferences\', {\n            method: \'POST\',\n            headers: { \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' },\n            body: JSON.stringify({ preferences: state.preferences })\n        }).catch(() => {});\n\n        // Go to review\n        const reviewIndex = cloudTree.findIndex(s => s.id === \'review\');\n        if (reviewIndex >= 0) showCloudStage(reviewIndex);\n    });\n}\n\n/* --- REVIEW / CART STAGE RENDERER ---------------------------------------- */\nfunction renderReviewStage(container) {\n    const totals = computeTotals();\n\n    const rows = Object.keys(state.preferences).map(key => {\n        const p = state.preferences[key];\n        // Find which stage index this came from\n        const stageIdx = cloudTree.findIndex(s => s.id === key);\n        return `\n            <tr class="review-row" data-stage-key="${key}" ${stageIdx >= 0 ? `data-stage-index="${stageIdx}"` : \'\'}>\n                <td class="review-sel-title">${p.title || key}</td>\n                <td class="review-sel-price">${p.price || \'—\'}</td>\n                <td class="review-sel-detail">${(p.details || \'\').substring(0, 90)}${p.details && p.details.length > 90 ? \'...\' : \'\'}</td>\n                <td class="review-sel-action">${stageIdx >= 0 ? \'<button class="review-edit-btn">✎ Edit</button>\' : \'\'}</td>\n            </tr>\n        `;\n    }).join(\'\');\n\n    container.innerHTML = `\n        <div class="cloud-stage-inner review-stage">\n            <div class="stage-header">\n                <div class="stage-icon">📋</div>\n                <h2>Review Your Configuration</h2>\n                <p class="stage-desc">Verify all selections before proceeding to the agreement. Click "Edit" to change any item.</p>\n            </div>\n            <div class="review-table-wrap">\n                <table class="review-table">\n                    <thead>\n                        <tr>\n                            <th>Selection</th>\n                            <th>Price</th>\n                            <th>Details</th>\n                            <th></th>\n                        </tr>\n                    </thead>\n                    <tbody>${rows || \'<tr><td colspan="4" style="text-align:center;color:#888;">No selections made yet.</td></tr>\'}</tbody>\n                </table>\n            </div>\n            <div class="review-totals-block">\n                <div class="review-total-line">\n                    <span class="rtl-label">Estimated One-Time Cost:</span>\n                    <span class="rtl-value">${totals.oneTimeMin === totals.oneTimeMax\n                        ? `$${totals.oneTimeMin.toLocaleString()} CAD`\n                        : `$${totals.oneTimeMin.toLocaleString()} – $${totals.oneTimeMax.toLocaleString()} CAD`}</span>\n                </div>\n                ${totals.monthlyMin > 0 || totals.monthlyMax > 0 ? `\n                <div class="review-total-line">\n                    <span class="rtl-label">Estimated Monthly Cost:</span>\n                    <span class="rtl-value">${totals.monthlyMin === totals.monthlyMax\n                        ? `$${totals.monthlyMin.toLocaleString()}/mo CAD`\n                        : `$${totals.monthlyMin.toLocaleString()} – $${totals.monthlyMax.toLocaleString()}/mo CAD`}</span>\n                </div>` : \'\'}\n                ${totals.hourly > 0 ? `\n                <div class="review-total-line">\n                    <span class="rtl-label">Hourly Services:</span>\n                    <span class="rtl-value">$${totals.hourly}/hour CAD (as needed)</span>\n                </div>` : \'\'}\n            </div>\n            <div class="review-actions">\n                <button class="btn-primary full-width" id="review-proceed-btn">\n                    ✓ Looks Good — Proceed to Agreement\n                </button>\n            </div>\n        </div>\n    `;\n\n    // Edit button handlers\n    container.querySelectorAll(\'.review-edit-btn\').forEach(btn => {\n        btn.addEventListener(\'click\', (e) => {\n            const row = e.target.closest(\'tr\');\n            const stageKey = row.dataset.stageKey;\n            const stageIdx = parseInt(row.dataset.stageIndex);\n\n            // Remove this and all subsequent selections\n            const histIdx = state.cloudHistory.findIndex(h => h.stageId === stageKey);\n            if (histIdx >= 0) {\n                const removed = state.cloudHistory.splice(histIdx);\n                removed.forEach(r => delete state.preferences[r.stageId]);\n            }\n            delete state.preferences[stageKey];\n\n            fetch(\'/api/preferences\', {\n                method: \'POST\',\n                headers: { \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' },\n                body: JSON.stringify({ preferences: state.preferences })\n            }).catch(() => {});\n\n            if (!isNaN(stageIdx) && stageIdx >= 0) {\n                showCloudStage(stageIdx);\n            }\n        });\n    });\n\n    // Proceed button\n    document.getElementById(\'review-proceed-btn\').addEventListener(\'click\', () => {\n        buildAndShowAgreement();\n    });\n}\n\n/* --- CLOUD OPTION HANDLER ------------------------------------------------ */\nfunction handleCloudOption(stageId, optionId) {\n    const stage = cloudTree.find(s => s.id === stageId);\n    if (!stage) return;\n    const selectedOption = stage.options.find(o => o.id === optionId);\n    if (!selectedOption) return;\n\n    // Store selection\n    state.preferences[stageId] = { ...selectedOption };\n\n    // History\n    state.cloudHistory.push({ stageId: stageId, stageIndex: state.currentStageIndex, optionId });\n\n    // Persist\n    fetch(\'/api/preferences\', {\n        method: \'POST\',\n        headers: { \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' },\n        body: JSON.stringify({ preferences: state.preferences })\n    }).catch(() => {});\n\n    // Navigate\n    const nextStageId = selectedOption.nextStage;\n    if (nextStageId === \'complete\') {\n        buildAndShowAgreement();\n    } else {\n        const nextIndex = cloudTree.findIndex(s => s.id === nextStageId);\n        if (nextIndex >= 0) showCloudStage(nextIndex);\n    }\n}\n\n// Back navigation\ndocument.getElementById(\'back-btn\').addEventListener(\'click\', () => {\n    if (state.cloudHistory.length > 0) {\n        const last = state.cloudHistory.pop();\n        delete state.preferences[last.stageId];\n        fetch(\'/api/preferences\', {\n            method: \'POST\',\n            headers: { \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' },\n            body: JSON.stringify({ preferences: state.preferences })\n        }).catch(() => {});\n        showCloudStage(last.stageIndex);\n    }\n});\n\n/* --- LANDING PAGE --------------------------------------------------------- */\nfunction handleNameEntry() {\n    const input = document.getElementById(\'name-input\');\n    const name = input ? input.value.trim() : \'\';\n    if (!name) { alert(\'Please enter your full name\'); return; }\n    state.userName = name;\n\n    fetch(\'/api/check-user\', {\n        method: \'POST\',\n        headers: { \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' },\n        body: JSON.stringify({ name })\n    })\n    .then(r => r.json())\n    .then(data => {\n        if (data.exists) {\n            const seal = document.getElementById(\'login-wax-seal\');\n            if (seal) seal.src = data.waxSeal || \'\';\n            showPage(\'login-page\');\n            initLoginSigPad();\n        } else {\n            showPage(\'password-page\');\n            startSealGeneration();\n        }\n    })\n    .catch(() => {\n        showPage(\'password-page\');\n        startSealGeneration();\n    });\n}\n\ndocument.getElementById(\'name-input\').addEventListener(\'keypress\', e => {\n    if (e.key === \'Enter\') handleNameEntry();\n});\ndocument.getElementById(\'enter-name-btn\').addEventListener(\'click\', handleNameEntry);\n\n/* --- REGISTRATION --------------------------------------------------------- */\nfunction startSealGeneration() {\n    const generating = document.getElementById(\'seal-generating\');\n    const form = document.getElementById(\'signature-password-form\');\n    const result = document.getElementById(\'wax-seal-result\');\n    if (generating) generating.style.display = \'flex\';\n    if (form) form.style.display = \'none\';\n    if (result) result.style.display = \'none\';\n\n    setTimeout(() => {\n        if (generating) generating.style.display = \'none\';\n        if (form) form.style.display = \'block\';\n        initRegisterSigPad();\n    }, 3000);\n}\n\n/* --- SIGNATURE PAD FACTORY ----------------------------------------------- */\nfunction createSigPad(canvas) {\n    const ctx = canvas.getContext(\'2d\');\n    ctx.strokeStyle = \'#1a1a2e\';\n    ctx.lineWidth = 2.2;\n    ctx.lineCap = \'round\';\n    ctx.lineJoin = \'round\';\n\n    let drawing = false;\n    let pts = [];\n    let lastX = 0, lastY = 0;\n\n    function coords(e) {\n        const r = canvas.getBoundingClientRect();\n        const src = e.touches ? e.touches[0] : e;\n        return [src.clientX - r.left, src.clientY - r.top];\n    }\n    function down(e) {\n        e.preventDefault();\n        drawing = true;\n        [lastX, lastY] = coords(e);\n        pts.push({ x: lastX, y: lastY, t: Date.now() });\n    }\n    function move(e) {\n        if (!drawing) return;\n        e.preventDefault();\n        const [x, y] = coords(e);\n        ctx.beginPath();\n        ctx.moveTo(lastX, lastY);\n        ctx.lineTo(x, y);\n        ctx.stroke();\n        [lastX, lastY] = [x, y];\n        pts.push({ x, y, t: Date.now() });\n    }\n    function up() { drawing = false; }\n\n    canvas.addEventListener(\'mousedown\', down);\n    canvas.addEventListener(\'mousemove\', move);\n    canvas.addEventListener(\'mouseup\', up);\n    canvas.addEventListener(\'mouseout\', up);\n    canvas.addEventListener(\'touchstart\', down, { passive: false });\n    canvas.addEventListener(\'touchmove\', move, { passive: false });\n    canvas.addEventListener(\'touchend\', up);\n\n    return {\n        clear() { ctx.clearRect(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height); pts = []; },\n        getData() { return pts.length > 8 ? pts : null; },\n        getImage() { return canvas.toDataURL(\'image/png\'); }\n    };\n}\n\nfunction initRegisterSigPad() {\n    const canvas = document.getElementById(\'register-signature-pad\');\n    if (!canvas) return;\n    state.registerSigPad = createSigPad(canvas);\n    document.getElementById(\'clear-register-signature\').addEventListener(\'click\', () => {\n        if (state.registerSigPad) state.registerSigPad.clear();\n    });\n}\n\nfunction initLoginSigPad() {\n    const canvas = document.getElementById(\'login-signature-pad\');\n    if (!canvas) return;\n    state.loginSigPad = createSigPad(canvas);\n    document.getElementById(\'clear-login-signature\').addEventListener(\'click\', () => {\n        if (state.loginSigPad) state.loginSigPad.clear();\n    });\n}\n\n/* --- CREATE ACCOUNT ------------------------------------------------------- */\ndocument.getElementById(\'create-account-btn\').addEventListener(\'click\', () => {\n    const pw = document.getElementById(\'password\').value;\n    const pw2 = document.getElementById(\'confirm-password\').value;\n    const err = document.getElementById(\'password-error\');\n    err.textContent = \'\';\n\n    if (pw) {\n        if (pw.length < 6) { err.textContent = \'Password must be at least 6 characters\'; return; }\n        if (!/[!@#$%^&*(),.?":{}|<>]/.test(pw)) { err.textContent = \'Password must include a special character\'; return; }\n        if (!/\\d/.test(pw)) { err.textContent = \'Password must include a number\'; return; }\n        if (pw !== pw2) { err.textContent = \'Passwords do not match\'; return; }\n    }\n\n    const sigData = state.registerSigPad ? state.registerSigPad.getData() : null;\n    if (!sigData) { err.textContent = \'Please sign to create your signature passkey\'; return; }\n\n    fetch(\'/api/register\', {\n        method: \'POST\',\n        headers: { \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' },\n        body: JSON.stringify({ name: state.userName, password: pw || null, confirmPassword: pw2 || null, signatureData: sigData })\n    })\n    .then(r => r.json())\n    .then(data => {\n        if (data.success) {\n            state.userToken = data.token;\n            state.waxSealImage = data.waxSeal;\n            document.getElementById(\'signature-password-form\').style.display = \'none\';\n            document.getElementById(\'wax-seal-result\').style.display = \'block\';\n            document.getElementById(\'user-wax-seal\').src = data.waxSeal;\n            document.getElementById(\'unique-token\').textContent = data.token;\n        } else {\n            err.textContent = data.error || \'Registration failed\';\n        }\n    })\n    .catch(() => { err.textContent = \'Network error — please try again\'; });\n});\n\ndocument.getElementById(\'continue-btn\').addEventListener(\'click\', () => {\n    showPage(\'cloud-page\');\n    showCloudStage(0);\n});\n\n/* --- LOGIN ---------------------------------------------------------------- */\ndocument.getElementById(\'show-password-login\').addEventListener(\'click\', () => {\n    const pwSection = document.getElementById(\'password-login-section\');\n    const visible = pwSection.style.display !== \'none\';\n    pwSection.style.display = visible ? \'none\' : \'block\';\n    state.usingPasswordBackup = !visible;\n});\n\ndocument.getElementById(\'login-btn\').addEventListener(\'click\', () => {\n    const nameEl = document.getElementById(\'login-name\');\n    const name = nameEl ? nameEl.value.trim() : state.userName;\n    const err = document.getElementById(\'login-error\');\n    const btn = document.getElementById(\'login-btn\');\n    err.textContent = \'\';\n\n    let sigData = null;\n    if (!state.usingPasswordBackup) {\n        sigData = state.loginSigPad ? state.loginSigPad.getData() : null;\n        if (!sigData) { err.textContent = \'Please sign to authenticate\'; return; }\n    }\n\n    const pw = state.usingPasswordBackup ? document.getElementById(\'login-password\').value : null;\n    if (!name) { err.textContent = \'Please enter your name\'; return; }\n\n    btn.textContent = \'Authenticating...\';\n    btn.disabled = true;\n\n    fetch(\'/api/login\', {\n        method: \'POST\',\n        headers: { \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' },\n        body: JSON.stringify({ name, password: pw, signatureData: sigData })\n    })\n    .then(r => r.json())\n    .then(data => {\n        btn.textContent = \'Authenticate\';\n        btn.disabled = false;\n        if (data.success) {\n            state.userName = name;\n            state.userToken = data.token;\n            state.waxSealImage = data.waxSeal;\n            loadPreferencesAndShowCloud();\n        } else {\n            err.textContent = data.error || \'Authentication failed\';\n            if (data.confidence !== undefined) {\n                err.textContent += ` (match: ${Math.round(data.confidence * 100)}%)`;\n            }\n        }\n    })\n    .catch(() => {\n        btn.textContent = \'Authenticate\';\n        btn.disabled = false;\n        err.textContent = \'Network error. Please try again.\';\n    });\n});\n\nfunction loadPreferencesAndShowCloud() {\n    fetch(\'/api/preferences\')\n        .then(r => r.json())\n        .then(data => {\n            state.preferences = ========================================================================== */\nfunction computeTotals() {\n    let oneTimeMin = 0, oneTimeMax = 0;\n    let monthlyMin = 0, monthlyMax = 0;\n    let hourly = 0;\n\n    // Accumulate from all preferences (except eta-rush and premiere-config handled separately)\n    Object.keys(state.preferences).forEach(key => {\n        if (key === \'eta-rush\' || key === \'premiere-config\') return;\n        const p = state.preferences[key];\n        oneTimeMin += (p.oneTimeMin || 0);\n        oneTimeMax += (p.oneTimeMax || 0);\n        monthlyMin += (p.monthlyMin || 0);\n        monthlyMax += (p.monthlyMax || 0);\n        if (p.hourly) hourly += p.hourly;\n    });\n\n    // ETA Rush surcharge (percentage of one-time cost)\n    const eta = state.preferences[\'eta-rush\'];\n    if (eta && eta.etaMultiplier && eta.etaMultiplier > 0) {\n        const surchargeMin = Math.round(oneTimeMin * eta.etaMultiplier);\n        const surchargeMax = Math.round(oneTimeMax * eta.etaMultiplier);\n        oneTimeMin += surchargeMin;\n        oneTimeMax += surchargeMax;\n    }\n\n    // Première Enterprise user billing\n    const premiere = state.preferences[\'premiere-config\'];\n    if (premiere) {\n        monthlyMin += (premiere.monthlyMin || 0);\n        monthlyMax += (premiere.monthlyMax || 0);\n    } else if (eta && (t.oneTimeMax > 0) {\n        if (t.oneTimeMin === t.oneTimeMax) {\n            parts.push(`$${t.oneTimeMin.toLocaleString()} CAD`);\n        } else {\n
